int fifo32_get(struct FIFO32 *fifo)
{
	if(fifo->free == fifo->size)
		return -1;
  281e6d:	b8 ff ff ff ff       	mov    $0xffffffff,%eax
	fifo->q++;
	if(fifo->q == fifo->size)
		fifo->q = 0;
	fifo->free++;
	return data;
}
